#
#   The following example data demonstrates an example of Azure environment.
#
#   In general, resources observed by the Azure observer consists of:
#
#   1) Subscription
#   2) Resource Group
#   3) Virtual Machine (VM)
#   4) VM's disk
#   5) VM's OS
#   6) VM's network interface
#   7) VM's network interface Security Group
#   8) Network interface's IP address
#   9) Virtual Network
#  10) Virtual Subnet
#
#
#   a) An Azure subscription contains a Resource Group
#   b) In each resource group, there are number of VM(s) assigned to it.
#   c) Each VM uses an operating system and disk
#   c) Each VM contains a network interface with an IP address and may belong to a network security group.
#   d) The IP address is part of a virtual subnet and the virtual subnet is part of a virtual network
#
#   To illustrate the above, let's choose a specific example:
#
#   a) Subscription 'GTS-IMI-Demo-EA-Resources-Dev/Ace' contains Resource Group 'mcms_mgmt_vg_customer-abc'
#   b) Resource Group 'mcms_mgmt_vg_customer-abc' has VM 'mcms_mgmt_jump_server' assigned to it.
#   c) VM 'mcms_mgmt_jump_server contains a network interface called 'mcms_mgmt_server_nic_0' with IP address '10.0.3.5'
#   d) IP address '10.0.3.5' is part of virtual subnet 'mgmt_vnet_customer-ACC-subnet'
#
#
